		//=================================================================================================================
		// Tutorial
		//=================================================================================================================

	"tutorial0_name"														"Allies"
	"tutorial0_text1"														"The main task of the players is to protect Roshan at all costs and destroy the concentration of Dark forces. To protect himself, Roshan built special protective structures around his lair and raised an army that would storm the enemy fortress every half a minute. All defensive towers can be improved by strengthening your defenses. To reinforce your army - free your allies from the clutches of neutral bosses."
	"tutorial1_name"														"Enemies"
	"tutorial1_text1"														"The Dark forces send out squads to attack Roshan every 30 seconds. Every 10 minutes, the forces of Darkness send especially strong warrior into battle - boss, each 3rd boss is an order of magnitude stronger than the others."
	"tutorial1_text2"														"The task of the Heroes is to destroy the Ice Throne and overthrow the King sitting on it. After that, the forces of Darkness will begin to attack from the home base."
	"tutorial1_text3"														"After the destruction of the Fortress of Darkness, the Dark Lord will go out on the battlefield. When the Dark Lord dies the game is over with the heroes winning."
	"tutorial2_name"														"Neutrals"
	"tutorial2_text1"														"There are neutral enemies on the map. They won't attack you or Roshan until you enter their territory or attack them."	
	"tutorial2_text2"														"Each location has its own ruler - a boss. Most neutral bosses have 3 forms. In 5 minutes after the death of the first, the second will appear and after his death, the third will appear - the final boss of the location."	
	"tutorial2_text3"														"In front of each location you can find signs that tell you about this location, the strength of the enemies inside it, about the artifacts and relics that can be found there as well as about potential secrets."
	"tutorial3_name"														"Quests"
	"tutorial3_text1"														"Pay attention to the allies who have an exclamation mark above their head. You can talk to these NPC and take the quests. You must disable the smart attack in order to open the quest."
	"tutorial4_name"														"Relics"
	"tutorial4_text1"														"The game contains special Relics. They are needed to create especially strong items. They can be gottten by killing the final versions of neutral bosses in different locations. You can see all the available relics and places where to find them by clicking on the Relics button."
	"tutorial5_name"														"Outworld"
	"tutorial5_text1"														"After finding the secret teleport, heroes will be able to enter to a special location - Outworld. This location is unique because there are no enemies in it. When you talk to the spirit of aganim you will be able to travel between different worlds. Worlds can be friendly, neutral and hostile."
	"tutorial6_name"														"Special objects"
	"tutorial6_text1"														"There are kinetic bridges in the game, standing on which the hero can overcome the abyss or mountain in no time. As well in the game there are special bridges that allow you to pass both above them and below them. Capture outposts to quickly move around the map. The outpost will be under your control for 10 minutes, after which it will need to be captured again."
